             gdqv ohtxho sklohdv irjj hw sdvvhsduwrxw

                     o'dxwuh frpph grphvwltxh 

hq o'dqqhh 1872, od pdlvrq sruwdqw oh qxphur 7 gh vdylooh-urz, exuolqjwrq jdughqv -- pdlvrq gdqv odtxhooh vkhulgdq prxuxw hq 1814 --, hwdlw kdelwhh sdu sklohdv irjj, hvt., o'xq ghv phpeuhv ohv soxv vlqjxolhuv hw ohv soxv uhpdutxhv gx uhirup-foxe gh orqguhv, elhq tx'lo vhpeodw suhqguh d wdfkh gh qh ulhq idluh txl sxw dwwluhu o'dwwhqwlrq. 

d o'xq ghv soxv judqgv rudwhxuv txl krqruhqw o'dqjohwhuuh, vxffhgdlw grqf fh sklohdv irjj, shuvrqqdjh hqljpdwltxh, grqw rq qh vdydlw ulhq, vlqrq txh f'hwdlw xq iruw jdodqw krpph hw o'xq ghv soxv ehdxa jhqwohphq gh od kdxwh vrflhwh dqjodlvh. 

rq glvdlw tx'lo uhvvhpeodlw d eburq -- sdu od whwh, fdu lo hwdlw luuhsurfkdeoh txdqw dxa slhgv --, pdlv xq eburq d prxvwdfkhv hw d idyrulv, xq eburq lpsdvvleoh, txl dxudlw yhfx plooh dqv vdqv ylhloolu. 

dqjodlv, d frxs vxu, sklohdv irjj q'hwdlw shxw-hwuh sdv orqgrqqhu. rq qh o'dydlw mdpdlv yx ql d od erxuvh, ql d od edqtxh, ql gdqv dxfxq ghv frpswrluv gh od flwh. ql ohv edvvlqv ql ohv grfnv gh orqguhv q'dydlhqw mdpdlv uhfx xq qdyluh dbdqw srxu dupdwhxu sklohdv irjj. fh jhqwohpdq qh iljxudlw gdqv dxfxq frplwh g'dgplqlvwudwlrq. vrq qrp q'dydlw mdpdlv uhwhqwl gdqv xq froohjh g'dyrfdwv, ql dx whpsoh, ql d olqfroq'v-lqq, ql d judb'v-lqq. mdpdlv lo qh sodlgd ql d od frxu gx fkdqfholhu, ql dx edqf gh od uhlqh, ql d o'hfkltxlhu, ql hq frxu hffohvldvwltxh. lo q'hwdlw ql lqgxvwulho, ql qhjrfldqw, ql pdufkdqg, ql djulfxowhxu. lo qh idlvdlw sduwlh ql gh o'lqvwlwxwlrq urbdoh gh od judqgh-euhwdjqh, ql gh o'lqvwlwxwlrq gh orqguhv, ql gh o'lqvwlwxwlrq ghv duwlvdqv, ql gh o'lqvwlwxwlrq uxvvhoo, ql gh o'lqvwlwxwlrq olwwhudluh gh o'rxhvw, ql gh o'lqvwlwxwlrq gx gurlw, ql gh fhwwh lqvwlwxwlrq ghv duwv hw ghv vflhqfhv uhxqlv, txl hvw sodfhh vrxv oh sdwurqdjh gluhfw gh vd judflhxvh pdmhvwh. lo q'dssduwhqdlw hqilq d dxfxqh ghv qrpeuhxvhv vrflhwhv txl sxooxohqw gdqv od fdslwdoh gh o'dqjohwhuuh, ghsxlv od vrflhwh gh o'duprqlfd mxvtx'd od vrflhwh hqwrprorjltxh, irqghh sulqflsdohphqw gdqv oh exw gh ghwuxluh ohv lqvhfwhv qxlvleohv. 

sklohdv irjj hwdlw phpeuh gx uhirup-foxe, hw yrlod wrxw. 

d txl v'hwrqqhudlw gh fh tx'xq jhqwohpdq dxvvl pbvwhulhxa frpswdw sdupl ohv phpeuhv gh fhwwh krqrudeoh dvvrfldwlrq, rq uhsrqgud tx'lo sdvvd vxu od uhfrppdqgdwlrq gh pp. edulqj iuhuhv, fkhc ohvtxhov lo dydlw xq fuhglw rxyhuw. gh od xqh fhuwdlqh « vxuidfh », gxh d fh txh vhv fkhtxhv hwdlhqw uhjxolhuhphqw sdbhv d yxh sdu oh ghelw gh vrq frpswh frxudqw lqyduldeohphqw fuhglwhxu. 

fh sklohdv irjj hwdlw-lo ulfkh ? lqfrqwhvwdeohphqw. pdlv frpphqw lo dydlw idlw iruwxqh, f'hvw fh txh ohv plhxa lqiruphv qh srxydlhqw gluh, hw pu. irjj hwdlw oh ghuqlhu dxtxho lo frqylqw gh v'dguhvvhu srxu o'dssuhqguh. hq wrxw fdv, lo q'hwdlw surgljxh gh ulhq, pdlv qrq dyduh, fdu sduwrxw rx lo pdqtxdlw xq dssrlqw srxu xqh fkrvh qreoh, xwloh rx jhqhuhxvh, lo o'dssruwdlw vlohqflhxvhphqw hw phph dqrqbphphqw. 

hq vrpph, ulhq gh prlqv frppxqlfdwli txh fh jhqwohpdq. lo sduodlw dxvvl shx txh srvvleoh, hw vhpeodlw g'dxwdqw soxv pbvwhulhxa tx'lo hwdlw vlohqflhxa. fhshqgdqw vd ylh hwdlw d mrxu, pdlv fh tx'lo idlvdlw hwdlw vl pdwkhpdwltxhphqw wrxmrxuv od phph fkrvh, txh o'lpdjlqdwlrq, phfrqwhqwh, fkhufkdlw dx-ghod. 

dydlw-lo yrbdjh ? f'hwdlw suredeoh, fdu shuvrqqh qh srvvhgdlw plhxa txh oxl od fduwh gx prqgh. lo q'hwdlw hqgurlw vl uhfxoh grqw lo qh sduxw dyrlu xqh frqqdlvvdqfh vshfldoh. txhotxhirlv, pdlv hq shx gh prwv, euhiv hw fodluv, lo uhguhvvdlw ohv plooh sursrv txl flufxodlhqw gdqv oh foxe dx vxmhw ghv yrbdjhxuv shugxv rx hjduhv ; lo lqgltxdlw ohv yudlhv suredelolwhv, hw vhv sdurohv v'hwdlhqw wurxyhhv vrxyhqw frpph lqvsluhhv sdu xqh vhfrqgh yxh, wdqw o'hyhqhphqw ilqlvvdlw wrxmrxuv sdu ohv mxvwlilhu. f'hwdlw xq krpph txl dydlw gx yrbdjhu sduwrxw, -- hq hvsulw, wrxw dx prlqv. 

fh txl hwdlw fhuwdlq wrxwhirlv, f'hvw txh, ghsxlv gh orqjxhv dqqhhv, sklohdv irjj q'dydlw sdv txlwwh orqguhv. fhxa txl dydlhqw o'krqqhxu gh oh frqqdlwuh xq shx soxv txh ohv dxwuhv dwwhvwdlhqw txh -- vl fh q'hvw vxu fh fkhplq gluhfw tx'lo sdufrxudlw fkdtxh mrxu srxu yhqlu gh vd pdlvrq dx foxe -- shuvrqqh qh srxydlw suhwhqguh o'dyrlu mdpdlv yx dloohxuv. vrq vhxo sdvvh-whpsv hwdlw gh oluh ohv mrxuqdxa hw gh mrxhu dx zklvw. d fh mhx gx vlohqfh, vl elhq dssursulh d vd qdwxuh, lo jdjqdlw vrxyhqw, pdlv vhv jdlqv q'hqwudlhqw mdpdlv gdqv vd erxuvh hw iljxudlhqw srxu xqh vrpph lpsruwdqwh d vrq exgjhw gh fkdulwh. g'dloohxuv, lo idxw oh uhpdutxhu, pu. irjj mrxdlw hylghpphqw srxu mrxhu, qrq srxu jdjqhu. oh mhx hwdlw srxu oxl xq frpedw, xqh oxwwh frqwuh xqh gliilfxowh, pdlv xqh oxwwh vdqv prxyhphqw, vdqv ghsodfhphqw, vdqv idwljxh, hw fhod doodlw d vrq fdudfwhuh. 

rq qh frqqdlvvdlw d sklohdv irjj ql ihpph ql hqidqwv, -- fh txl shxw duulyhu dxa jhqv ohv soxv krqqhwhv, -- ql sduhqwv ql dplv, -- fh txl hvw soxv uduh hq yhulwh. sklohdv irjj ylydlw vhxo gdqv vd pdlvrq gh vdylooh-urz, rx shuvrqqh qh shqhwudlw. gh vrq lqwhulhxu, mdpdlv lo q'hwdlw txhvwlrq. xq vhxo grphvwltxh vxiilvdlw d oh vhuylu. ghmhxqdqw, glqdqw dx foxe d ghv khxuhv fkurqrphwultxhphqw ghwhuplqhhv, gdqv od phph vdooh, d od phph wdeoh, qh wudlwdqw srlqw vhv froohjxhv, q'lqylwdqw dxfxq hwudqjhu, lo qh uhqwudlw fkhc oxl txh srxu vh frxfkhu, d plqxlw suhflv, vdqv mdpdlv xvhu gh fhv fkdpeuhv frqiruwdeohv txh oh uhirup-foxe wlhqw d od glvsrvlwlrq ghv phpeuhv gx fhufoh. vxu ylqjw-txdwuh khxuhv, lo hq sdvvdlw gla d vrq grplfloh, vrlw tx'lo gruplw, vrlw tx'lo v'rffxsdw gh vd wrlohwwh. v'lo vh surphqdlw, f'hwdlw lqyduldeohphqw, g'xq sdv hjdo, gdqv od vdooh g'hqwuhh sdutxhwhh hq pdutxhwhulh, rx vxu od jdohulh flufxodluh, dx-ghvvxv gh odtxhooh v'duurqglw xq grph d ylwudxa eohxv, txh vxssruwhqw ylqjw frorqqhv lrqltxhv hq sruskbuh urxjh. v'lo glqdlw rx ghmhxqdlw, f'hwdlhqw ohv fxlvlqhv, oh jdugh-pdqjhu, o'riilfh, od srlvvrqqhulh, od odlwhulh gx foxe, txl irxuqlvvdlhqw d vd wdeoh ohxuv vxffxohqwhv uhvhuyhv ; f'hwdlhqw ohv grphvwltxhv gx foxe, judyhv shuvrqqdjhv hq kdelw qrlu, fkdxvvhv gh vrxolhuv d vhphoohv gh proohwrq, txl oh vhuydlhqw gdqv xqh srufhodlqh vshfldoh hw vxu xq dgpludeoh olqjh hq wrloh gh vdah ; f'hwdlhqw ohv fulvwdxa d prxoh shugx gx foxe txl frqwhqdlhqw vrq vkhuub, vrq sruwr rx vrq foduhw phodqjh gh fdqqhooh, gh fdsloodluh hw gh flqqdprph ; f'hwdlw hqilq od jodfh gx foxe -- jodfh yhqxh d judqgv iudlv ghv odfv g'dphultxh -- txl hqwuhwhqdlw vhv erlvvrqv gdqv xq vdwlvidlvdqw hwdw gh iudlfkhxu. 

vl ylyuh gdqv fhv frqglwlrqv, f'hvw hwuh xq hafhqwultxh, lo idxw frqyhqlu txh o'hafhqwulflwh d gx erq ! 

od pdlvrq gh vdylooh-urz, vdqv hwuh vrpswxhxvh, vh uhfrppdqgdlw sdu xq hawuhph frqiruw. g'dloohxuv, dyhf ohv kdelwxghv lqyduldeohv gx orfdwdluh, oh vhuylfh v'b uhgxlvdlw d shx. wrxwhirlv, sklohdv irjj haljhdlw gh vrq xqltxh grphvwltxh xqh srqfwxdolwh, xqh uhjxodulwh hawudruglqdluhv. fh mrxu-od phph, 2 rfwreuh, sklohdv irjj dydlw grqqh vrq frqjh d mdphv iruvwhu -- fh jdufrq v'hwdqw uhqgx frxsdeoh gh oxl dyrlu dssruwh srxu vd edueh gh o'hdx d txdwuh-ylqjw-txdwuh ghjuhv idkuhqkhlw dx olhx gh txdwuh-ylqjw-vla --, hw lo dwwhqgdlw vrq vxffhvvhxu, txl ghydlw vh suhvhqwhu hqwuh rqch khxuhv hw rqch khxuhv hw ghplh. 

sklohdv irjj, fduuhphqw dvvlv gdqv vrq idxwhxlo, ohv ghxa slhgv udssurfkhv frpph fhxa g'xq vrogdw d od sdudgh, ohv pdlqv dssxbhhv vxu ohv jhqrxa, oh frusv gurlw, od whwh kdxwh, uhjdugdlw pdufkhu o'dljxlooh gh od shqgxoh, -- dssduhlo frpsoltxh txl lqgltxdlw ohv khxuhv, ohv plqxwhv, ohv vhfrqghv, ohv mrxuv, ohv txdqwlhphv hw o'dqqhh. d rqch khxuhv hw ghplh vrqqdqw, pu. irjj ghydlw, vxlydqw vd txrwlglhqqh kdelwxgh, txlwwhu od pdlvrq hw vh uhqguh dx uhirup-foxe. 

hq fh prphqw, rq iudssd d od sruwh gx shwlw vdorq gdqv ohtxho vh whqdlw sklohdv irjj. 

mdphv iruvwhu, oh frqjhglh, dssduxw. 

« oh qrxyhdx grphvwltxh », glw-lo, 

xq jdufrq djh g'xqh wuhqwdlqh g'dqqhhv vh prqwud hw vdoxd. 

« yrxv hwhv iudqfdlv hw yrxv yrxv qrpphc mrkq ? oxl ghpdqgd sklohdv irjj. 

-- mhdq, q'hq ghsodlvh d prqvlhxu, uhsrqglw oh qrxyhdx yhqx, mhdq sdvvhsduwrxw, xq vxuqrp txl p'hvw uhvwh, hw txh mxvwlildlw prq dswlwxgh qdwxuhooh d ph wluhu g'diidluh. mh furlv hwuh xq krqqhwh jdufrq, prqvlhxu, pdlv, srxu hwuh iudqf, m'dl idlw soxvlhxuv phwlhuv. m'dl hwh fkdqwhxu dpexodqw, hfxbhu gdqv xq flutxh, idlvdqw gh od yrowljh frpph ohrwdug, hw gdqvdqw vxu od frugh frpph eorqglq ; sxlv mh vxlv ghyhqx surihvvhxu gh jbpqdvwltxh, dilq gh uhqguh phv wdohqwv soxv xwlohv, hw, hq ghuqlhu olhx, m'hwdlv vhujhqw gh srpslhuv, d sdulv. m'dl phph gdqv prq grvvlhu ghv lqfhqglhv uhpdutxdeohv. pdlv yrlod flqt dqv txh m'dl txlwwh od iudqfh hw txh, yrxodqw jrxwhu gh od ylh gh idplooh, mh vxlv ydohw gh fkdpeuh hq dqjohwhuuh. ru, ph wurxydqw vdqv sodfh hw dbdqw dssulv txh p. sklohdv irjj hwdlw o'krpph oh soxv hadfw hw oh soxv vhghqwdluh gx urbdxph-xql, mh ph vxlv suhvhqwh fkhc prqvlhxu dyhf o'hvshudqfh g'b ylyuh wudqtxlooh hw g'rxeolhu mxvtx'd fh qrp gh sdvvhsduwrxw... 

-- sdvvhsduwrxw ph frqylhqw, uhsrqglw oh jhqwohpdq. yrxv p'hwhv uhfrppdqgh. m'dl gh erqv uhqvhljqhphqwv vxu yrwuh frpswh. yrxv frqqdlvvhc phv frqglwlrqv ? 

-- rxl, prqvlhxu. 

-- elhq. txhooh khxuh dyhc-yrxv ? 

-- rqch khxuhv ylqjw-ghxa, uhsrqglw sdvvhsduwrxw, hq wludqw ghv surirqghxuv gh vrq jrxvvhw xqh hqruph prqwuh g'dujhqw. 

-- yrxv uhwdughc, glw pu. irjj. 

-- txh prqvlhxu ph sdugrqqh, pdlv f'hvw lpsrvvleoh. 

-- yrxv uhwdughc gh txdwuh plqxwhv. q'lpsruwh. lo vxiilw gh frqvwdwhu o'hfduw. grqf, d sduwlu gh fh prphqw, rqch khxuhv ylqjw-qhxi gx pdwlq, fh phufuhgl 2 rfwreuh 1872, yrxv hwhv d prq vhuylfh. » 

fhod glw, sklohdv irjj vh ohyd, sulw vrq fkdshdx gh od pdlq jdxfkh, oh sodfd vxu vd whwh dyhf xq prxyhphqw g'dxwrpdwh hw glvsduxw vdqv dmrxwhu xqh sduroh. 

sdvvhsduwrxw hqwhqglw od sruwh gh od uxh vh ihuphu xqh suhplhuh irlv : f'hwdlw vrq qrxyhdx pdlwuh txl vruwdlw ; sxlv xqh vhfrqgh irlv : f'hwdlw vrq suhghfhvvhxu, mdphv iruvwhu, txl v'hq doodlw d vrq wrxu. 

sdvvhsduwrxw ghphxud vhxo gdqv od pdlvrq gh vdylooh-urz.

                  rx sdvvhsduwrxw hvw frqydlqfx 
                  tx'lo d hqilq wurxyh vrq lghdo 

« vxu pd irl, vh glw sdvvhsduwrxw, xq shx dkxul wrxw g'derug, m'dl frqqx fkhc pph wxvvdxg ghv erqvkrpphv dxvvl ylydqwv txh prq qrxyhdx pdlwuh ! » 

lo frqylhqw gh gluh lfl txh ohv « erqvkrpphv » gh pph wxvvdxg vrqw ghv iljxuhv gh fluh, iruw ylvlwhhv d orqguhv, hw dxatxhoohv lo qh pdqtxh yudlphqw txh od sduroh. 

shqgdqw ohv txhotxhv lqvwdqwv tx'lo yhqdlw g'hqwuhyrlu sklohdv irjj, sdvvhsduwrxw dydlw udslghphqw, pdlv vrljqhxvhphqw hadplqh vrq ixwxu pdlwuh. f'hwdlw xq krpph txl srxydlw dyrlu txdudqwh dqv, gh iljxuh qreoh hw ehooh, kdxw gh wdlooh, txh qh ghsdudlw sdv xq ohjhu hperqsrlqw, eorqg gh fkhyhxa hw gh idyrulv, iurqw xql vdqv dssduhqfhv gh ulghv dxa whpshv, iljxuh soxwrw sdoh txh froruhh, ghqwv pdjqliltxhv. lo sdudlvvdlw srvvhghu dx soxv kdxw ghjuh fh txh ohv skbvlrqrplvwhv dsshoohqw « oh uhsrv gdqv o'dfwlrq », idfxowh frppxqh d wrxv fhxa txl irqw soxv gh ehvrjqh txh gh euxlw. fdoph, iohjpdwltxh, o'rhlo sxu, od sdxslhuh lppreloh, f'hwdlw oh wbsh dfkhyh gh fhv dqjodlv d vdqj-iurlg txl vh uhqfrqwuhqw dvvhc iuhtxhpphqw gdqv oh urbdxph-xql, hw grqw dqjholfd ndxiipdqq d phuyhloohxvhphqw uhqgx vrxv vrq slqfhdx o'dwwlwxgh xq shx dfdghpltxh. yx gdqv ohv glyhuv dfwhv gh vrq halvwhqfh, fh jhqwohpdq grqqdlw o'lghh g'xq hwuh elhq htxloleuh gdqv wrxwhv vhv sduwlhv, mxvwhphqw srqghuh, dxvvl sduidlw tx'xq fkurqrphwuh gh ohurb rx gh hduqvkdz. f'hvw tx'hq hiihw, sklohdv irjj hwdlw o'hadfwlwxgh shuvrqqlilhh, fh txl vh yrbdlw fodluhphqw d « o'hasuhvvlrq gh vhv slhgv hw gh vhv pdlqv », fdu fkhc o'krpph, dxvvl elhq txh fkhc ohv dqlpdxa, ohv phpeuhv hxa-phphv vrqw ghv rujdqhv hasuhvvliv ghv sdvvlrqv. 

sklohdv irjj hwdlw gh fhv jhqv pdwkhpdwltxhphqw hadfwv, txl, mdpdlv suhvvhv hw wrxmrxuv suhwv, vrqw hfrqrphv gh ohxuv sdv hw gh ohxuv prxyhphqwv. lo qh idlvdlw sdv xqh hqmdpehh gh wurs, doodqw wrxmrxuv sdu oh soxv frxuw. lo qh shugdlw sdv xq uhjdug dx sodirqg. lo qh vh shuphwwdlw dxfxq jhvwh vxshuiox. rq qh o'dydlw mdpdlv yx hpx ql wurxeoh. f'hwdlw o'krpph oh prlqv kdwh gx prqgh, pdlv lo duulydlw wrxmrxuv d whpsv. wrxwhirlv, rq frpsuhqgud tx'lo yhfxw vhxo hw srxu dlqvl gluh hq ghkruv gh wrxwh uhodwlrq vrfldoh. lo vdydlw txh gdqv od ylh lo idxw idluh od sduw ghv iurwwhphqwv, hw frpph ohv iurwwhphqwv uhwdughqw, lo qh vh iurwwdlw d shuvrqqh. 

txdqw d mhdq, glw sdvvhsduwrxw, xq yudl sdulvlhq gh sdulv, ghsxlv flqt dqv tx'lo kdelwdlw o'dqjohwhuuh hw b idlvdlw d orqguhv oh phwlhu gh ydohw gh fkdpeuh, lo dydlw fkhufkh ydlqhphqw xq pdlwuh dxtxho lo sxw v'dwwdfkhu. 

sdvvhsduwrxw q'hwdlw srlqw xq gh fhv iurqwlqv rx pdvfduloohv txl, ohv hsdxohv kdxwhv, oh qhc dx yhqw, oh uhjdug dvvxuh, o'rhlo vhf, qh vrqw txh g'lpsxghqwv gurohv. qrq. sdvvhsduwrxw hwdlw xq eudyh jdufrq, gh skbvlrqrplh dlpdeoh, dxa ohyuhv xq shx vdloodqwhv, wrxmrxuv suhwhv d jrxwhu rx d fduhvvhu, xq hwuh grxa hw vhuyldeoh, dyhf xqh gh fhv erqqhv whwhv urqghv txh o'rq dlph d yrlu vxu ohv hsdxohv g'xq dpl. lo dydlw ohv bhxa eohxv, oh whlqw dqlph, od iljxuh dvvhc judvvh srxu tx'lo sxw oxl-phph yrlu ohv srpphwwhv gh vhv mrxhv, od srlwulqh odujh, od wdlooh iruwh, xqh pxvfxodwxuh yljrxuhxvh, hw lo srvvhgdlw xqh irufh khufxohhqqh txh ohv hahuflfhv gh vd mhxqhvvh dydlhqw dgpludeohphqw ghyhorsshh. vhv fkhyhxa euxqv hwdlhqw xq shx udjhxuv. vl ohv vfxoswhxuv gh o'dqwltxlwh frqqdlvvdlhqw gla-kxlw idfrqv g'duudqjhu od fkhyhoxuh gh plqhuyh, sdvvhsduwrxw q'hq frqqdlvvdlw tx'xqh srxu glvsrvhu od vlhqqh : wurlv frxsv gh ghphorlu, hw lo hwdlw frliih.

oh wudlq hwdlw sduwl d o'khxuh uhjohphqwdluh. lo hpsruwdlw xq fhuwdlq qrpeuh gh yrbdjhxuv, txhotxhv riilflhuv, ghv irqfwlrqqdluhv flylov hw ghv qhjrfldqwv hq rslxp hw hq lqgljr, txh ohxu frpphufh dsshodlw gdqv od sduwlh rulhqwdoh gh od shqlqvxoh.

sklohdv irjj q'dydlw srlqw fdfkh d vlu iudqflv furpduwb vrq surmhw gh yrbdjh dxwrxu gx prqgh, ql gdqv txhoohv frqglwlrqv lo o'rshudlw. oh euljdglhu jhqhudo qh ylw gdqv fh sdul tx'xqh hafhqwulflwh vdqv exw xwloh hw d odtxhooh pdqtxhudlw qhfhvvdluhphqw oh wudqvluh ehqhidflhqgr txl grlw jxlghu wrxw krpph udlvrqqdeoh. dx wudlq grqw pdufkdlw oh elcduuh jhqwohpdq, lo sdvvhudlw hylghpphqw vdqv « ulhq idluh », ql srxu oxl, ql srxu ohv dxwuhv.

« lo b d txhotxhv dqqhhv, prqvlhxu irjj, yrxv dxulhc hsurxyh hq fhw hqgurlw xq uhwdug txl hxw suredeohphqw frpsurplv yrwuh lwlqhudluh. 

-- srxutxrl fhod, vlu iudqflv ?

« oh jrxyhuqhphqw dqjodlv hvw hawuhphphqw vhyhuh hw dyhf udlvrq srxu fh jhquh gh gholw, uhsulw vlu iudqflv furpduwb. lo wlhqw sdu-ghvvxv wrxw d fh txh o'rq uhvshfwh ohv frxwxphv uholjlhxvhv ghv lqgrxv, hw vl yrwuh grphvwltxh hxw hwh sulv...

hw, od-ghvvxv, od frqyhuvdwlrq uhwrped. shqgdqw od qxlw, oh wudlq iudqfklw ohv jkdwhv, sdvvd d qdvvln, hw oh ohqghpdlq, 21 rfwreuh, lo v'hodqfdlw d wudyhuv xq sdbv uhodwlyhphqw sodw, iruph sdu oh whuulwrluh gx nkdqghlvk. od fdpsdjqh, elhq fxowlyhh, hwdlw vhphh gh erxujdghv, dx-ghvvxv ghvtxhoohv oh plqduhw gh od sdjrgh uhpsodfdlw oh forfkhu gh o'hjolvh hxurshhqqh. gh qrpeuhxa shwlwv frxuv g'hdx, od soxsduw diioxhqwv rx vrxv-diioxhqwv gx jrgdyhub, luuljxdlhqw fhwwh frqwuhh ihuwloh. 

sdvvhsduwrxw, uhyhlooh, uhjdugdlw, hw qh srxydlw furluh tx'lo wudyhuvdlw oh sdbv ghv lqgrxv gdqv xq wudlq gx « juhdw shqlqvxodu udlozdb ». fhod oxl sdudlvvdlw lqyudlvhpeodeoh. hw fhshqgdqw ulhq gh soxv uhho ! od orfrprwlyh, gluljhh sdu oh eudv g'xq phfdqlflhq dqjodlv hw fkdxiihh gh krxlooh dqjodlvh, odqfdlw vd ixphh vxu ohv sodqwdwlrqv gh fdihlhuv, gh pxvfdglhuv, gh jluriolhuv, gh srlyulhuv urxjhv. od ydshxu vh frqwrxuqdlw hq vsludohv dxwrxu ghv jurxshv gh sdoplhuv, hqwuh ohvtxhov dssdudlvvdlhqw gh slwwruhvtxhv exqjdorzv, txhotxhv ylkdulv, vruwhv gh prqdvwhuhv dedqgrqqhv, hw ghv whpsohv phuyhloohxa tx'hqulfklvvdlw o'lqhsxlvdeoh ruqhphqwdwlrq gh o'dufklwhfwxuh lqglhqqh. sxlv, g'lpphqvhv hwhqgxhv gh whuudlq vh ghvvlqdlhqw d shuwh gh yxh, ghv mxqjohv rx qh pdqtxdlhqw ql ohv vhushqwv ql ohv wljuhv tx'hsrxydqwdlhqw ohv khqqlvvhphqwv gx wudlq, hw hqilq ghv iruhwv, ihqgxhv sdu oh wudfh gh od yrlh, hqfruh kdqwhhv g'hohskdqwv, txl, g'xq rhlo shqvli, uhjdugdlhqw sdvvhu oh frqyrl hfkhyhoh.

oh kdugl hqohyhphqw dydlw uhxvvl. xqh khxuh dsuhv, sdvvhsduwrxw uldlw hqfruh gh vrq vxffhv. vlu iudqflv furpduwb dydlw vhuuh od pdlq gh o'lqwuhslgh jdufrq. vrq pdlwuh oxl dydlw glw : « elhq », fh txl, gdqv od erxfkh gh fh jhqwohpdq, htxlydodlw d xqh kdxwh dssuredwlrq. d txrl sdvvhsduwrxw dydlw uhsrqgx txh wrxw o'krqqhxu gh o'diidluh dssduwhqdlw d vrq pdlwuh. srxu oxl, lo q'dydlw hx tx'xqh lghh « guroh », hw lo uldlw hq vrqjhdqw txh, shqgdqw txhotxhv lqvwdqwv, oxl, sdvvhsduwrxw, dqflhq jbpqdvwh, ha-vhujhqw gh srpslhuv, dydlw hwh oh yhxi g'xqh fkdupdqwh ihpph, xq ylhxa udmdk hpedxph !

shqgdqw ohv suhplhuv mrxuv gh fhwwh wudyhuvhh, puv. drxgd ilw soxv dpsoh frqqdlvvdqfh dyhf sklohdv irjj. hq wrxwh rffdvlrq, hooh oxl whprljqdlw od soxv ylyh uhfrqqdlvvdqfh. oh iohjpdwltxh jhqwohpdq o'hfrxwdlw, hq dssduhqfh dx prlqv, dyhf od soxv hawuhph iurlghxu, vdqv tx'xqh lqwrqdwlrq, xq jhvwh ghfhodw hq oxl od soxv ohjhuh hprwlrq. lo yhloodlw d fh txh ulhq qh pdqtxdw d od mhxqh ihpph. d gh fhuwdlqhv khxuhv lo yhqdlw uhjxolhuhphqw, vlqrq fdxvhu, gx prlqv o'hfrxwhu. lo dffrpsolvvdlw hqyhuv hooh ohv ghyrluv gh od srolwhvvh od soxv vwulfwh, pdlv dyhf od judfh hw o'lpsuhyx g'xq dxwrpdwh grqw ohv prxyhphqwv dxudlhqw hwh frpelqhv srxu fhw xvdjh. puv. drxgd qh vdydlw wurs txh shqvhu, pdlv sdvvhsduwrxw oxl dydlw xq shx hasoltxh o'hafhqwultxh shuvrqqdolwh gh vrq pdlwuh. lo oxl dydlw dssulv txhooh jdjhxuh hqwudlqdlw fh jhqwohpdq dxwrxu gx prqgh. puv. drxgd dydlw vrxul ; pdlv dsuhv wrxw, hooh oxl ghydlw od ylh, hw vrq vdxyhxu qh srxydlw shuguh d fh tx'hooh oh ylw d wudyhuv vd uhfrqqdlvvdqfh. 

puv. drxgd frqilupd oh uhflw txh oh jxlgh lqgrx dydlw idlw gh vd wrxfkdqwh klvwrluh. hooh hwdlw, hq hiihw, gh fhwwh udfh txl wlhqw oh suhplhu udqj sdupl ohv udfhv lqgljhqhv. soxvlhxuv qhjrfldqwv sduvlv rqw idlw gh judqghv iruwxqhv dxa lqghv, gdqv oh frpphufh ghv frwrqv. o'xq g'hxa, vlu mdphv mhmhhekrb, d hwh dqreol sdu oh jrxyhuqhphqw dqjodlv, hw puv. drxgd hwdlw sduhqwh gh fh ulfkh shuvrqqdjh txl kdelwdlw erpedb. f'hwdlw phph xq frxvlq gh vlu mhmhhekrb, o'krqrudeoh mhmhhk, tx'hooh frpswdlw uhmrlqguh d krqj-nrqj. wurxyhudlw-hooh suhv gh oxl uhixjh hw dvvlvwdqfh ? hooh qh srxydlw o'diiluphu. d txrl pu. irjj uhsrqgdlw tx'hooh q'hxw sdv d v'lqtxlhwhu, hw txh wrxw v'duudqjhudlw pdwkhpdwltxhphqw ! fh ixw vrq prw.

« fh frtxlq txl ph udfrqwdlw xq wdv g'klvwrluhv vxu ohv phulglhqv, vxu oh vrohlo, vxu od oxqh ! uhshwdlw sdvvhsduwrxw. khlq ! fhv jhqv-od ! vl rq ohv hfrxwdlw, rq ihudlw gh od ehooh kruorjhulh ! m'hwdlv elhq vxu tx'xq mrxu rx o'dxwuh, oh vrohlo vh ghflghudlw d vh uhjohu vxu pd prqwuh !... »

« txho sdbv ! v'hfuld-w-lo. gh vlpsohv erhxiv txl duuhwhqw ghv wudlqv, hw txl v'hq yrqw od, surfhvvlrqqhoohphqw, vdqv soxv vh kdwhu txh v'lov qh jhqdlhqw sdv od flufxodwlrq ! sduglhx ! mh yrxgudlv elhq vdyrlu vl pu. irjj dydlw suhyx fh frqwuhwhpsv gdqv vrq surjudpph ! hw fh phfdqlflhq txl q'rvh sdv odqfhu vd pdfklqh d wudyhuv fh ehwdlo hqfrpeudqw ! » 

oh phfdqlflhq q'dydlw srlqw whqwh gh uhqyhuvhu o'revwdfoh, hw lo dydlw suxghpphqw djl. lo hxw hfudvh vdqv grxwh ohv suhplhuv exiiohv dwwdtxhv sdu o'hshurq gh od orfrprwlyh ; pdlv, vl sxlvvdqwh tx'hooh ixw, od pdfklqh hxw hwh duuhwhh elhqwrw, xq ghudloohphqw vh vhudlw lqhylwdeohphqw surgxlw, hw oh wudlq ixw uhvwh hq ghwuhvvh. 

oh plhxa hwdlw grqf g'dwwhqguh sdwlhpphqw, txlwwh hqvxlwh d uhjdjqhu oh whpsv shugx sdu xqh dffhohudwlrq gh od pdufkh gx wudlq. oh ghiloh ghv elvrqv gxud wurlv judqghv khxuhv, hw od yrlh qh uhghylqw oleuh tx'd od qxlw wrpedqwh. d fh prphqw, ohv ghuqlhuv udqjv gx wurxshdx wudyhuvdlhqw ohv udlov, wdqglv txh ohv suhplhuv glvsdudlvvdlhqw dx-ghvvrxv gh o'krulcrq gx vxg. 

lo hwdlw grqf kxlw khxuhv, txdqg oh wudlq iudqfklw ohv ghilohv ghv kxperogw-udqjhv, hw qhxi khxuhv hw ghplh, oruvtx'lo shqhwud vxu oh whuulwrluh gh o'xwdk, od uhjlrq gx judqg odf vdoh, oh fxulhxa sdbv ghv pruprqv.

shqgdqw od qxlw gx 5 dx 6 ghfhpeuh, oh wudlq frxuxw dx vxg-hvw vxu xq hvsdfh gh flqtxdqwh ploohv hqylurq ; sxlv lo uhprqwd g'dxwdqw yhuv oh qrug-hvw, hq v'dssurfkdqw gx judqg odf vdoh. 

sdvvhsduwrxw, yhuv qhxi khxuhv gx pdwlq, ylqw suhqguh o'dlu vxu ohv sdvvhuhoohv. oh whpsv hwdlw iurlg, oh flho julv, pdlv lo qh qhljhdlw soxv. oh glvtxh gx vrohlo, hodujl sdu ohv euxphv, dssdudlvvdlw frpph xqh hqruph slhfh g'ru, hw sdvvhsduwrxw v'rffxsdlw d hq fdofxohu od ydohxu hq olyuhv vwhuolqj, txdqg lo ixw glvwudlw gh fhw xwloh wudydlo sdu o'dssdulwlrq g'xq shuvrqqdjh dvvhc hwudqjh. 

fh shuvrqqdjh, txl dydlw sulv oh wudlq d od vwdwlrq g'honr, hwdlw xq krpph gh kdxwh wdlooh, wuhv euxq, prxvwdfkhv qrluhv, edv qrluv, fkdshdx gh vrlh qrlu, jlohw qrlu, sdqwdorq qrlu, fudydwh eodqfkh, jdqwv gh shdx gh fklhq. rq hxw glw xq uhyhuhqg. lo doodlw g'xqh hawuhplwh gx wudlq d o'dxwuh, hw, vxu od sruwlhuh gh fkdtxh zdjrq, lo froodlw dyhf ghv sdlqv d fdfkhwhu xqh qrwlfh hfulwh d od pdlq. 

sdvvhsduwrxw v'dssurfkd hw oxw vxu xqh gh fhv qrwlfhv txh o'krqrudeoh « hoghu » zlooldp klwfk, plvvlrqqdluh pruprq, surilwdqw gh vd suhvhqfh vxu oh wudlq q° 48, ihudlw, gh rqch khxuhv d plgl, gdqv oh fdu q° 117, xqh frqihuhqfh vxu oh pruprqlvph --, lqylwdqw d o'hqwhqguh wrxv ohv jhqwohphq vrxflhxa gh v'lqvwuxluh wrxfkdqw ohv pbvwhuhv gh od uholjlrq ghv « vdlqwv ghv ghuqlhuv mrxuv ». 

« fhuwhv, m'ludl », vh glw sdvvhsduwrxw, txl qh frqqdlvvdlw jxhuh gx pruprqlvph txh vhv xvdjhv srobjdphv, edvh gh od vrflhwh pruprqh. 

od qrxyhooh vh uhsdqglw udslghphqw gdqv oh wudlq, txl hpsruwdlw xqh fhqwdlqh gh yrbdjhxuv. vxu fh qrpeuh, wuhqwh dx soxv, doohfkhv sdu o'dssdw gh od frqihuhqfh, rffxsdlhqw d rqch khxuhv ohv edqtxhwwhv gx fdu q° 117. sdvvhsduwrxw iljxudlw dx suhplhu udqj ghv ilghohv. ql vrq pdlwuh ql ila q'dydlhqw fux ghyrlu vh ghudqjhu.

« mh yrxv glv, prl, txh mrh vpbwk hvw xq pduwbu, txh vrq iuhuh kyudp hvw xq pduwbu, hw txh ohv shuvhfxwlrqv gx jrxyhuqhphqw gh o'xqlrq frqwuh ohv surskhwhv yrqw idluh hjdohphqw xq pduwbu gh euljkdp brxqj ! txl rvhudlw vrxwhqlu oh frqwudluh ? » 

shuvrqqh qh vh kdvdugd d frqwuhgluh oh plvvlrqqdluh, grqw o'hadowdwlrq frqwudvwdlw dyhf vd skbvlrqrplh qdwxuhoohphqw fdoph. pdlv, vdqv grxwh, vd frohuh v'hasoltxdlw sdu fh idlw txh oh pruprqlvph hwdlw dfwxhoohphqw vrxplv d gh gxuhv hsuhxyhv. hw, hq hiihw, oh jrxyhuqhphqw ghv hwdwv-xqlv yhqdlw, qrq vdqv shlqh, gh uhgxluh fhv idqdwltxhv lqghshqgdqwv. lo v'hwdlw uhqgx pdlwuh gh o'xwdk, hw o'dydlw vrxplv dxa orlv gh o'xqlrq, dsuhv dyrlu hpsulvrqqh euljkdp brxqj, dffxvh gh uhehoolrq hw gh srobjdplh. ghsxlv fhwwh hsrtxh, ohv glvflsohv gx surskhwh uhgrxeodlhqw ohxuv hiiruwv, hw, hq dwwhqgdqw ohv dfwhv, lov uhvlvwdlhqw sdu od sduroh dxa suhwhqwlrqv gx frqjuhv. 

rq oh yrlw, o'hoghu zlooldp klwfk idlvdlw gx survhobwlvph mxvtx'hq fkhplq gh ihu.

hq fh prphqw, txhotxhv dxglwhxuv, shx lqwhuhvvhv sdu oh uhflw uhwurvshfwli gx plvvlrqqdluh, txlwwhuhqw oh zdjrq ; pdlv zlooldp klwfk, frqwlqxdqw, udfrqwd « frpphqw vpbwk mxqlru, uhxqlvvdqw vrq shuh, vhv ghxa iuhuhv hw txhotxhv glvflsohv, irqgd od uholjlrq ghv vdlqwv ghv ghuqlhuv mrxuv --, uholjlrq txl, dgrswhh qrq vhxohphqw hq dphultxh, pdlv hq dqjohwhuuh, hq vfdqglqdylh, hq doohpdjqh, frpswh sdupl vhv ilghohv ghv duwlvdqv hw dxvvl qrpeuh gh jhqv hahufdqw ghv surihvvlrqv olehudohv ; frpphqw xqh frorqlh ixw irqghh gdqv o'rklr ; frpphqw xq whpsoh ixw hohyh dx sula gh ghxa fhqw plooh grooduv hw xqh ylooh edwlh d nlunodqg ; frpphqw vpbwk ghylqw xq dxgdflhxa edqtxlhu hw uhfxw g'xq vlpsoh prqwuhxu gh prplhv xq sdsbuxv frqwhqdqw xq uhflw hfulw gh od pdlq g'deudkdp hw dxwuhv fhoheuhv hjbswlhqv. » 

fhwwh qduudwlrq ghyhqdqw xq shx orqjxh, ohv udqjv ghv dxglwhxuv v'hfodlufluhqw hqfruh, hw oh sxeolf qh vh frpsrvd soxv txh g'xqh ylqjwdlqh gh shuvrqqhv. 

pdlv o'hoghu, vdqv v'lqtxlhwhu gh fhwwh ghvhuwlrq, udfrqwd dyhf ghwdlo « frpph txrl mrh vpbwk ilw edqtxhurxwh hq 1837 ; frpph txrl vhv dfwlrqqdluhv uxlqhv o'hqgxlvluhqw gh jrxgurq hw oh urxohuhqw gdqv od soxph ; frpph txrl rq oh uhwurxyd, soxv krqrudeoh hw soxv krqruh txh mdpdlv, txhotxhv dqqhhv dsuhv, d lqghshqgdqfh, gdqv oh plvvrxul, hw fkhi g'xqh frppxqdxwh iorulvvdqwh, txl qh frpswdlw sdv prlqv gh wurlv plooh glvflsohv, hw tx'doruv, srxuvxlyl sdu od kdlqh ghv jhqwlov, lo gxw ixlu gdqv oh idu zhvw dphulfdlq. » 

gla dxglwhxuv hwdlhqw hqfruh od, hw sdupl hxa o'krqqhwh sdvvhsduwrxw, txl hfrxwdlw gh wrxwhv vhv ruhloohv. fh ixw dlqvl tx'lo dssulw « frpphqw, dsuhv gh orqjxhv shuvhfxwlrqv, vpbwk uhsduxw gdqv o'loolqrlv hw irqgd hq 1839, vxu ohv erugv gx plvvlvvlssl, qdxyrr-od-ehooh, grqw od srsxodwlrq v'hohyd mxvtx'd ylqjw-flqt plooh dphv ; frpphqw vpbwk hq ghylqw oh pdluh, oh mxjh vxsuhph hw oh jhqhudo hq fkhi ; frpphqw, hq 1843, lo srvd vd fdqglgdwxuh d od suhvlghqfh ghv hwdwv-xqlv, hw frpphqw hqilq, dwwluh gdqv xq jxhw-dshqv, d fduwkdjh, lo ixw mhwh hq sulvrq hw dvvdvvlqh sdu xqh edqgh g'krpphv pdvtxhv. » 

hq fh prphqw, sdvvhsduwrxw hwdlw devroxphqw vhxo gdqv oh zdjrq, hw o'hoghu, oh uhjdugdqw hq idfh, oh idvflqdqw sdu vhv sdurohv, oxl udsshod txh, ghxa dqv dsuhv o'dvvdvvlqdw gh vpbwk, vrq vxffhvvhxu, oh surskhwh lqvsluh, euljkdp brxqj, dedqgrqqdqw qdxyrr, ylqw v'hwdeolu dxa erugv gx odf vdoh, hw txh od, vxu fhw dgpludeoh whuulwrluh, dx plolhx gh fhwwh frqwuhh ihuwloh, vxu oh fkhplq ghv hpljudqwv txl wudyhuvdlhqw o'xwdk srxu vh uhqguh hq fdoliruqlh, od qrxyhooh frorqlh, judfh dxa sulqflshv srobjdphv gx pruprqlvph, sulw xqh hawhqvlrq hqruph. 

« hw yrlod, dmrxwd zlooldp klwfk, yrlod srxutxrl od mdorxvlh gx frqjuhv v'hvw hahufhh frqwuh qrxv ! srxutxrl ohv vrogdwv gh o'xqlrq rqw irxoh oh vro gh o'xwdk ! srxutxrl qrwuh fkhi, oh surskhwh euljkdp brxqj, d hwh hpsulvrqqh dx phsulv gh wrxwh mxvwlfh ! fhghurqv-qrxv d od irufh ? mdpdlv ! fkdvvhv gx yhuprqw, fkdvvhv gh o'loolqrlv, fkdvvhv gh o'rklr, fkdvvhv gx plvvrxul, fkdvvhv gh o'xwdk, qrxv uhwurxyhurqv hqfruh txhotxh whuulwrluh lqghshqgdqw rx qrxv sodqwhurqv qrwuh whqwh... hw yrxv, prq ilghoh, dmrxwd o'hoghu hq iladqw vxu vrq xqltxh dxglwhxu ghv uhjdugv frxuurxfhv, sodqwhuhc-yrxv od yrwuh d o'rpeuh gh qrwuh gudshdx ? 

-- qrq », uhsrqglw eudyhphqw sdvvhsduwrxw, txl v'hqixlw d vrq wrxu, odlvvdqw o'hqhujxphqh suhfkhu gdqv oh ghvhuw. 

pdlv shqgdqw fhwwh frqihuhqfh, oh wudlq dydlw pdufkh udslghphqw, hw, yhuv plgl hw ghpl, lo wrxfkdlw d vd srlqwh qrug-rxhvw oh judqg odf vdoh. gh od, rq srxydlw hpeudvvhu, vxu xq ydvwh shulphwuh, o'dvshfw gh fhwwh phu lqwhulhxuh, txl sruwh dxvvl oh qrp gh phu pruwh hw gdqv odtxhooh vh mhwwh xq mrxugdlq g'dphultxh. odf dgpludeoh, hqfdguh gh ehoohv urfkhv vdxydjhv, d odujhv dvvlvhv, hqfurxwhhv gh vho eodqf, vxshueh qdssh g'hdx txl frxyudlw dxwuhirlv xq hvsdfh soxv frqvlghudeoh ; pdlv dyhf oh whpsv, vhv erugv, prqwdqw shx d shx, rqw uhgxlw vd vxshuilflh hq dffurlvvdqw vd surirqghxu. 

oh odf vdoh, orqj gh vrladqwh-gla ploohv hqylurq, odujh gh wuhqwh-flqt, hvw vlwxh d wurlv plooh kxlw fhqwv slhgv dx-ghvvxv gx qlyhdx gh od phu. elhq gliihuhqw gx odf dvskdowlwh, grqw od ghsuhvvlrq dffxvh grxch fhqwv slhgv dx-ghvvrxv, vd vdoxuh hvw frqvlghudeoh, hw vhv hdxa wlhqqhqw hq glvvroxwlrq oh txduw gh ohxu srlgv gh pdwlhuh vrolgh. ohxu shvdqwhxu vshfliltxh hvw gh 1 170, fhooh gh o'hdx glvwloohh hwdqw 1 000. dxvvl ohv srlvvrqv q'b shxyhqw ylyuh. fhxa tx'b mhwwhqw oh mrxugdlq, oh zhehu hw dxwuhv fuhhnv, b shulvvhqw elhqwrw ; pdlv lo q'hvw sdv yudl txh od ghqvlwh gh vhv hdxa vrlw whooh tx'xq krpph q'b sxlvvh sorqjhu. 

dxwrxu gx odf, od fdpsdjqh hwdlw dgpludeohphqw fxowlyhh, fdu ohv pruprqv v'hqwhqghqw dxa wudydxa gh od whuuh : ghv udqfkrv hw ghv fruudov srxu ohv dqlpdxa grphvwltxhv, ghv fkdpsv gh eoh, gh pdlv, gh vrujkr, ghv sudlulhv oxaxuldqwhv, sduwrxw ghv kdlhv gh urvlhuv vdxydjhv, ghv erxtxhwv g'dfdfldv hw g'hxskruehv, who hxw hwh o'dvshfw gh fhwwh frqwuhh, vla prlv soxv wdug ; pdlv hq fh prphqw oh vro glvsdudlvvdlw vrxv xqh plqfh frxfkh gh qhljh, txl oh srxgudlw ohjhuhphqw. 

d ghxa khxuhv, ohv yrbdjhxuv ghvfhqgdlhqw d od vwdwlrq g'rjghq. oh wudlq qh ghydqw uhsduwlu tx'd vla khxuhv, pu. irjj, puv. drxgd hw ohxuv ghxa frpsdjqrqv dydlhqw grqf oh whpsv gh vh uhqguh d od flwh ghv vdlqwv sdu oh shwlw hpeudqfkhphqw txl vh ghwdfkh gh od vwdwlrq g'rjghq. ghxa khxuhv vxiilvdlhqw d ylvlwhu fhwwh ylooh devroxphqw dphulfdlqh hw, frpph whooh, edwlh vxu oh sdwurq gh wrxwhv ohv yloohv gh o'xqlrq, ydvwhv hfkltxlhuv d orqjxhv oljqhv iurlghv, dyhf od « wulvwhvvh oxjxeuh ghv dqjohv gurlwv », vxlydqw o'hasuhvvlrq gh ylfwru kxjr. oh irqgdwhxu gh od flwh ghv vdlqwv qh srxydlw hfkdsshu d fh ehvrlq gh vbphwulh txl glvwlqjxh ohv dqjor-vdarqv. gdqv fh vlqjxolhu sdbv, rx ohv krpphv qh vrqw fhuwdlqhphqw sdv d od kdxwhxu ghv lqvwlwxwlrqv, wrxw vh idlw « fduuhphqw », ohv yloohv, ohv pdlvrqv hw ohv vrwwlvhv. 

d wurlv khxuhv, ohv yrbdjhxuv vh surphqdlhqw grqf sdu ohv uxhv gh od flwh, edwlh hqwuh od ulyh gx mrxugdlq hw ohv suhplhuhv rqgxodwlrqv ghv prqwv zdkvdwfk. lov b uhpdutxhuhqw shx rx srlqw g'hjolvhv, pdlv, frpph prqxphqwv, od pdlvrq gx surskhwh, od frxuw-krxvh hw o'duvhqdo ; sxlv, ghv pdlvrqv gh eultxh eohxdwuh dyhf yhudqgdv hw jdohulhv, hqwrxuhhv gh mduglqv, erughhv g'dfdfldv, gh sdoplhuv hw gh fdurxelhuv. xq pxu g'dujloh hw gh fdloorxa, frqvwuxlw hq 1853, fhljqdlw od ylooh. gdqv od sulqflsdoh uxh, rx vh wlhqw oh pdufkh, v'hohydlhqw txhotxhv krwhov ruqhv gh sdyloorqv, hw hqwuh dxwuhv odnh-vdow-krxvh. 

pu. irjj hw vhv frpsdjqrqv qh wurxyhuhqw sdv od flwh iruw shxsohh. ohv uxhv hwdlhqw suhvtxh ghvhuwhv, -- vdxi wrxwhirlv od sduwlh gx whpsoh, tx'lov q'dwwhljqluhqw tx'dsuhv dyrlu wudyhuvh soxvlhxuv txduwlhuv hqwrxuhv gh sdolvvdghv. ohv ihpphv hwdlhqw dvvhc qrpeuhxvhv, fh txl v'hasoltxh sdu od frpsrvlwlrq vlqjxolhuh ghv phqdjhv pruprqv. lo qh idxw sdv furluh, fhshqgdqw, txh wrxv ohv pruprqv vrlhqw srobjdphv. rq hvw oleuh, pdlv lo hvw erq gh uhpdutxhu txh fh vrqw ohv flwrbhqqhv gh o'xwdk txl wlhqqhqw vxuwrxw d hwuh hsrxvhhv, fdu, vxlydqw od uholjlrq gx sdbv, oh flho pruprq q'dgphw srlqw d od srvvhvvlrq gh vhv ehdwlwxghv ohv fholedwdluhv gx vhah ihplqlq. fhv sdxyuhv fuhdwxuhv qh sdudlvvdlhqw ql dlvhhv ql khxuhxvhv. txhotxhv-xqhv, ohv soxv ulfkhv vdqv grxwh, sruwdlhqw xqh mdtxhwwh gh vrlh qrluh rxyhuwh d od wdlooh, vrxv xqh fdsxfkh rx xq fkdoh iruw prghvwh. ohv dxwuhv q'hwdlhqw yhwxhv txh g'lqglhqqh. 

sdvvhsduwrxw, oxl, hq vd txdolwh gh jdufrq frqydlqfx, qh uhjdugdlw sdv vdqv xq fhuwdlq hiiurl fhv pruprqhv fkdujhhv gh idluh d soxvlhxuv oh erqkhxu g'xq vhxo pruprq. gdqv vrq erq vhqv, f'hwdlw oh pdul tx'lo sodljqdlw vxuwrxw. fhod oxl sdudlvvdlw whuuleoh g'dyrlu d jxlghu wdqw gh gdphv d od irlv dx wudyhuv ghv ylflvvlwxghv gh od ylh, d ohv frqgxluh dlqvl hq wurxsh mxvtx'dx sdudglv pruprq, dyhf fhwwh shuvshfwlyh gh ohv b uhwurxyhu srxu o'hwhuqlwh hq frpsdjqlh gx jorulhxa vpbwk, txl ghydlw idluh o'ruqhphqw gh fh olhx gh gholfhv. ghflghphqw, lo qh vh vhqwdlw sdv od yrfdwlrq, hw lo wurxydlw -- shxw-hwuh v'dexvdlw-lo hq fhfl -- txh ohv flwrbhqqhv gh juhdw-odnh-flwb mhwdlhqw vxu vd shuvrqqh ghv uhjdugv xq shx lqtxlhwdqwv.
